#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: semua_data1
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS semua_data1;

CREATE TABLE `semua_data1` (
  `id_semua_data` bigint(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,

  PRIMARY KEY (`id_semua_data`),
  KEY `id_admin` (`id_admin`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=3501 DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;
